# IPC to HTTP/WS Migration Implementation Plan

> **For agentic workers:** REQUIRED SUB-SKILL: Use `superpowers:subagent-driven-development` (recommended) or `superpowers:executing-plans` to implement this plan task-by-task. Steps use checkbox (`- [ ]`) syntax for tracking.

**Goal:** Migrate Hive from Electron IPC-backed application APIs to a T3Code-style local HTTP/WebSocket backend, leaving Electron as a desktop shell only.

**Architecture:** Hive will gain a `src/server` runtime that owns database, git, filesystem, terminal, script, agent, settings, telemetry, and streaming services. The renderer will connect over authenticated HTTP/WS through a typed client. Electron IPC will shrink to a small `desktopBridge` for native shell functions only.

**Tech Stack:** Electron, React/Vite, TypeScript, Node HTTP/WebSocket runtime, Zod schemas, Vitest, Playwright, existing Hive service modules.

---

## Desired End State

Hive should run in two equivalent UI hosts:

- Electron desktop app: Electron starts and supervises a local backend server, then loads the renderer.
- Chrome/browser app: a browser loads the same renderer and connects to an already-running Hive backend.

The backend server owns all high-privilege app behavior:

- SQLite database access
- project/worktree operations
- git operations and watchers
- file tree scanning and file reads/writes
- attachment storage
- terminal PTYs
- script execution
- bash execution
- OpenCode, Claude Code, Claude CLI, and Codex session management
- agent streaming events, approvals, questions, plan approvals, and command approvals
- usage/account/settings/telemetry operations
- ticket import and kanban operations

Electron IPC remains only for native desktop shell capabilities:

- native folder/file picker
- native context menu
- app/window/menu actions
- updater
- open external URL/path
- app quit/restart
- secure desktop bootstrap
- desktop-only overlays and native UI integrations

## Non-Goals

- Do not rewrite the renderer UI.
- Do not replace Electron packaging.
- Do not expose the server publicly by default.
- Do not make Ghostty native surfaces browser-compatible.
- Do not delete the current IPC bridge until HTTP/WS parity exists.
- Do not move every renderer call site in one commit.

## Migration Strategy

Use a strangler migration.

1. Introduce a server and renderer HTTP/WS client.
2. Add a compatibility shim that exposes the existing `window.db`, `window.gitOps`, `window.opencodeOps`, and related APIs over HTTP/WS.
3. Migrate one domain at a time from IPC to RPC.
4. Keep old IPC handlers calling the same extracted services until each domain has parity.
5. Move renderer call sites from globals to explicit imported clients after the system works.
6. Delete old IPC surfaces only after all direct callers are gone.

This avoids a risky one-shot rewrite of the renderer, preload, and main process.

## Canonical Transport Shape

Define a shared request/response/event model in `src/shared/rpc`.

```ts
export interface RpcRequest {
  id: string
  method: string
  params: unknown
}

export type RpcResponse =
  | { id: string; ok: true; value: unknown }
  | {
      id: string
      ok: false
      error: {
        code: string
        message: string
        details?: unknown
      }
    }

export interface ServerEvent {
  channel: string
  payload: unknown
}
```

During the compatibility phase, convert RPC responses back into the existing `Envelope<T>` shape at the renderer compatibility boundary. That keeps current stores/components stable while transport changes underneath.

## Proposed File Structure

Create these new areas:

```text
src/server/
  bin.ts
  config.ts
  server.ts
  auth/
    bootstrap.ts
    session.ts
  events/
    event-bus.ts
  routes/
    environment.ts
    auth.ts
    static.ts
    attachments.ts
  rpc/
    protocol.ts
    router.ts
    ws-server.ts
    domains/
      db.ts
      project.ts
      worktree.ts
      git.ts
      file-tree.ts
      file.ts
      attachment.ts
      agent.ts
      terminal.ts
      script.ts
      bash.ts
      settings.ts
      connection.ts
      kanban.ts
      ticket-import.ts
      usage.ts
      account.ts
      telemetry.ts
      diagnostics.ts

src/shared/rpc/
  envelope.ts
  methods.ts
  events.ts
  errors.ts

src/renderer/src/api/
  environment.ts
  auth-bootstrap.ts
  hive-client.ts
  ws-transport.ts
  desktop-bridge.ts

src/main/desktop/
  backend-config.ts
  backend-manager.ts
  desktop-bridge-handlers.ts
```

Existing IPC handlers should be retained temporarily, then deleted domain by domain.

---

## Phase 1: Server Skeleton

**Goal:** Create a standalone Hive backend process with a health route and minimal WebSocket RPC.

**Files:**

- Create: `src/server/config.ts`
- Create: `src/server/bin.ts`
- Create: `src/server/server.ts`
- Create: `src/server/events/event-bus.ts`
- Create: `src/server/rpc/protocol.ts`
- Create: `src/server/rpc/router.ts`
- Create: `src/server/rpc/ws-server.ts`
- Create: `src/shared/rpc/envelope.ts`
- Create: `src/shared/rpc/errors.ts`
- Test: `src/server/__tests__/server-config.test.ts`
- Test: `src/server/__tests__/server-smoke.test.ts`
- Test: `src/server/__tests__/rpc-router.test.ts`

- [x] Add `ServerConfig` with `mode`, `host`, `port`, `baseDir`, `devUrl`, `staticDir`, `desktopBootstrapToken`, `logLevel`, and path derivation.
- [x] Add a server entrypoint that can run without Electron.
- [x] Add `GET /.well-known/hive/environment`.
- [x] Add `/ws` WebSocket endpoint.
- [x] Add `system.ping` RPC returning `{ ok: true }`.
- [x] Add typed RPC error conversion for validation errors, domain errors, and unexpected defects.
- [x] Add server event bus with `publish`, `subscribe`, and `unsubscribe`.
- [x] Verify that `pnpm exec vitest run src/server/__tests__/server-smoke.test.ts` passes.

**Acceptance criteria:**

- The server can start without creating an Electron window.
- A client can hit the health route.
- A client can call `system.ping` over WebSocket.

---

## Phase 2: Desktop Backend Manager

**Goal:** Make Electron start and supervise the backend server before opening the renderer.

**Files:**

- Create: `src/main/desktop/backend-config.ts`
- Create: `src/main/desktop/backend-manager.ts`
- Create: `src/main/desktop/backend-manager.test.ts`
- Modify: `src/main/index.ts`
- Modify: `src/preload/index.ts`

- [x] Add backend port selection, defaulting to `3773` and scanning upward when unavailable.
- [x] Generate a one-time desktop bootstrap token per Electron run.
- [x] Spawn the backend with `ELECTRON_RUN_AS_NODE=1`.
- [x] Pass bootstrap config to the child process through a file descriptor or a scoped environment variable.
- [x] Capture backend stdout/stderr to Hive logs.
- [x] Poll `/.well-known/hive/environment` until ready.
- [x] Open the renderer only after backend readiness.
- [x] Add bounded restart on unexpected backend exit.
- [x] Stop backend on app shutdown.

**Acceptance criteria:**

- `pnpm dev` starts a backend process first.
- The Electron window opens only after backend readiness.
- Backend crash logs are visible.
- The backend shuts down when Electron quits.

---

## Phase 3: Desktop Bridge

**Goal:** Shrink Electron preload toward native shell features while keeping the old IPC namespaces temporarily.

**Files:**

- Create: `src/main/desktop/desktop-bridge-handlers.ts`
- Create: `src/renderer/src/api/desktop-bridge.ts`
- Modify: `src/preload/index.ts`
- Modify: `src/preload/index.d.ts`

Final stable preload surface:

```ts
export interface DesktopBridge {
  getLocalEnvironmentBootstrap(): Promise<LocalEnvironmentBootstrap | null>
  getPathForFile(file: File): string
}
```

- [x] Add `window.desktopBridge`.
- [x] Keep existing `window.db`, `window.gitOps`, and similar namespaces for compatibility.
- [x] Route native folder picking through `desktopBridge.pickFolder(options?)`, and make `projectApi.openDirectoryDialog()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the RPC compatibility method while preserving the existing nullable selected-path result.
- [x] Route native update checks through `desktopBridge.checkForUpdate(options?)`, and make `updaterApi.checkForUpdate()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the RPC compatibility method while preserving manual-check option forwarding and void completion.
- [x] Route native update downloads through `desktopBridge.downloadUpdate()`, and make `updaterApi.downloadUpdate()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the RPC compatibility method while preserving void completion.
- [x] Route native update installs through `desktopBridge.installUpdate()`, and make `updaterApi.installUpdate()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the RPC compatibility method while preserving void completion.
- [x] Route native update channel switching through `desktopBridge.setUpdateChannel(channel)`, and make `updaterApi.setChannel(channel)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the RPC compatibility method while preserving channel argument forwarding.
- [x] Route native update version lookup through `desktopBridge.getUpdaterVersion()`, and make `updaterApi.getVersion()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the RPC compatibility method while preserving the string version value.
- [x] Route native menu state updates through `desktopBridge.updateMenuState(state)`, and make `systemApi.updateMenuState(state)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the RPC compatibility method while preserving menu enablement flags.
- [x] Route native project icon picking through `desktopBridge.pickProjectIcon(projectId)`, and make `projectApi.pickProjectIcon(projectId)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the RPC compatibility method while preserving the `{ success, filename?, error? }` result shape.
- [x] Route default external URL opening through `desktopBridge.openExternal(url)`, and make `systemApi.openInChrome(url)` prefer that desktop bridge when no custom browser command is provided while preserving the `systemOps.openInChrome` RPC fallback for custom commands.
- [x] Route custom-command browser opening through `desktopBridge.openInChrome(url, customCommand?)`, while preserving the `systemOps.openInChrome` RPC fallback for browser-only and compatibility flows.
- [x] Route native external app opening through `desktopBridge.openInApp(appName, path)`, and make `systemApi.openInApp(appName, path)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving `{ success, error? }`.
- [x] Route native confirmation dialogs through `desktopBridge.confirm(message)`, and make `systemApi.confirm(message)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to `window.confirm(message)` while preserving boolean OK/cancel semantics.
- [x] Route native application menu actions through `desktopBridge.onMenuAction(listener)`, and make `systemApi.onMenuAction(channel, callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to WebSocket menu event subscriptions while preserving per-channel filtering.
- [x] Route native updater checking notifications through `desktopBridge.onUpdaterChecking(listener)`, and make `updaterApi.onChecking(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `updater:checking` event while preserving callback-only semantics.
- [x] Route native updater-available notifications through `desktopBridge.onUpdaterAvailable(listener)`, and make `updaterApi.onUpdateAvailable(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `updater:available` event while preserving payload validation on the fallback path.
- [x] Route native updater-not-available notifications through `desktopBridge.onUpdaterNotAvailable(listener)`, and make `updaterApi.onUpdateNotAvailable(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `updater:not-available` event while preserving payload validation on the fallback path.
- [x] Route native updater progress notifications through `desktopBridge.onUpdaterProgress(listener)`, and make `updaterApi.onProgress(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `updater:progress` event while preserving payload validation on the fallback path.
- [x] Route native updater downloaded notifications through `desktopBridge.onUpdaterDownloaded(listener)`, and make `updaterApi.onUpdateDownloaded(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `updater:downloaded` event while preserving payload validation on the fallback path.
- [x] Route native updater error notifications through `desktopBridge.onUpdaterError(listener)`, and make `updaterApi.onError(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `updater:error` event while preserving payload validation on the fallback path.
- [x] Route native new-session shortcut notifications through `desktopBridge.onNewSessionShortcut(listener)`, and make `systemApi.onNewSessionShortcut(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `shortcut:new-session` event while preserving callback-only semantics.
- [x] Route native close-session shortcut notifications through `desktopBridge.onCloseSessionShortcut(listener)`, and make `systemApi.onCloseSessionShortcut(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `shortcut:close-session` event while preserving callback-only semantics.
- [x] Route native file-search shortcut notifications through `desktopBridge.onFileSearchShortcut(listener)`, and make `systemApi.onFileSearchShortcut(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `shortcut:file-search` event while preserving callback-only semantics.
- [x] Route native quit-confirmation-show notifications through `desktopBridge.onQuitConfirmationShow(listener)`, and make `systemApi.onQuitConfirmationShow(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `shortcut:quit-confirmation-show` event while preserving callback-only semantics.
- [x] Route native quit-confirmation-hide notifications through `desktopBridge.onQuitConfirmationHide(listener)`, and make `systemApi.onQuitConfirmationHide(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `shortcut:quit-confirmation-hide` event while preserving callback-only semantics.
- [x] Route native edit-paste menu notifications through `desktopBridge.onEditPaste(listener)`, and make `systemApi.onEditPaste(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `edit:paste` event while preserving string-payload validation on the fallback path.
- [x] Route native window-focused notifications through `desktopBridge.onWindowFocused(listener)`, and make `systemApi.onWindowFocused(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `app:windowFocused` event while preserving callback-only semantics.
- [x] Route native notification navigation events through `desktopBridge.onNotificationNavigate(listener)`, and make `systemApi.onNotificationNavigate(callback)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to the WebSocket `notification:navigate` event while preserving payload validation on the fallback path.
- [x] Route native app quit requests through `desktopBridge.quitApp()`, and make `systemApi.quitApp()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving void completion.
- [x] Route native keep-awake power-save-blocker requests through `desktopBridge.setKeepAwake(active)`, and make `systemApi.setKeepAwake(active)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving boolean active forwarding.
- [x] Route native packaged-mode checks through `desktopBridge.isPackaged()`, and make `systemApi.isPackaged()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving the boolean app-packaged result.
- [x] Route native response-log mode checks through `desktopBridge.isLogMode()`, and make `systemApi.isLogMode()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving the `--log` flag result.
- [x] Route native agent SDK detection through `desktopBridge.detectAgentSdks()`, and make `systemApi.detectAgentSdks()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving `{ opencode, claude, codex }`.
- [x] Route native platform checks through `desktopBridge.getPlatform()`, and make `systemApi.getPlatform()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving the Node platform string result.
- [x] Route native log-directory lookups through `desktopBridge.getLogDir()`, and make `systemApi.getLogDir()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving the log directory string.
- [x] Route native app-path lookups through `desktopBridge.getAppPaths()`, and make `systemApi.getAppPaths()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving `{ userData, home, logs }`.
- [x] Route native app-version lookups through `desktopBridge.getAppVersion()`, and make `systemApi.getAppVersion()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving the version string.
- [x] Route native reveal-in-folder actions through `desktopBridge.showItemInFolder(path)`, and make `projectApi.showInFolder(path)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving void completion.
- [x] Route native default-app path opening through `desktopBridge.openPath(path)`, and make `projectApi.openPath(path)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving void completion for renderer callers.
- [x] Route native clipboard writes through `desktopBridge.writeClipboardText(text)`, and make `projectApi.copyToClipboard(text)` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving void completion.
- [x] Route native clipboard reads through `desktopBridge.readClipboardText()`, and make `projectApi.readFromClipboard()` prefer that desktop bridge before falling back to RPC for browser/compatibility mode while preserving the string clipboard result.
- [x] Finalize native dialog/menu/updater routing through renderer RPC and backend desktop commands instead of expanding `desktopBridge`; keep `desktopBridge` limited to backend bootstrap and file path extraction.
- [x] Move desktop-only types away from core server/shared RPC types.

**Acceptance criteria:**

- Native menu, folder picker, updater, and external URL actions still work.
- Renderer can read backend bootstrap information from `desktopBridge`.

## Phase 4: Renderer HTTP/WS Client

**Goal:** Add a browser-capable renderer client and a compatibility shim for the existing global APIs.

**Files:**

- Create: `src/renderer/src/api/environment.ts`
- Create: `src/renderer/src/api/auth-bootstrap.ts`
- Create: `src/renderer/src/api/ws-transport.ts`
- Create: `src/renderer/src/api/hive-client.ts`
- Removed after renderer startup and production code no longer used compatibility globals: `src/renderer/src/api/legacy-window-api.ts`
- Test: `src/renderer/src/api/__tests__/environment.test.ts`
- Test: `src/renderer/src/api/__tests__/hive-client.test.ts`
- Removed after startup stopped installing the shim: `src/renderer/src/api/__tests__/legacy-window-api.test.ts`

- [x] Resolve backend target from `desktopBridge.getLocalEnvironmentBootstrap()`.
- [x] Resolve backend target from Vite env for browser dev mode.
- [x] Resolve backend target from `window.location.origin` for production browser mode.
- [x] Exchange desktop bootstrap token for an authenticated session.
- [x] Create reconnecting WebSocket transport.
- [x] Implement `HiveClient.request(method, params)`.
- [x] Implement `HiveClient.subscribe(channel, params, callback)`.
- [x] Implement `installLegacyWindowApi(client)` that recreates the existing preload global namespaces.
- [x] Remove `installLegacyWindowApi(client)` and `legacy-window-api.ts` after explicit renderer API modules replaced compatibility globals.

- [x] Add WebSocket subscription coverage for `opencode:stream`, proving subscribed clients receive backend event-bus OpenCode stream payloads with session IDs, child session IDs, status payloads, and arbitrary stream data on the local server event channel without any preload IPC listener or `webContents.send` bridge.

**Acceptance criteria:**

- Renderer code can call `window.db.setting.get` through the compatibility shim.
- A browser tab can connect to a local backend in dev mode.

---

## Phase 5: Authentication

**Goal:** Protect the local backend even before remote access exists.

**Files:**

- Create: `src/server/auth/bootstrap.ts`
- Create: `src/server/auth/session.ts`
- Create: `src/server/routes/auth.ts`
- Modify: `src/server/rpc/ws-server.ts`
- Test: `src/server/__tests__/auth-bootstrap.test.ts`
- Test: `src/server/__tests__/auth-ws.test.ts`

- [x] Add `POST /api/auth/bootstrap` to exchange a desktop bootstrap token.
- [x] Add `GET /api/auth/session` to check auth state.
- [x] Add `POST /api/auth/ws-token` to issue a short-lived WS token.
- [x] Require auth for WebSocket upgrade.
- [x] Require auth for high-privilege HTTP routes.
- [x] Allow unauthenticated access only to health/environment and bootstrap endpoints.

**Acceptance criteria:**

- Unauthenticated WS connection is rejected.
- Desktop bootstrap token creates an authenticated session.
- Browser mode can authenticate when given valid pairing/bootstrap credentials.

**Goal:** Prove the migration pattern with stateful but lower-risk domains.

**Domains:**

- `db`
- `settingsOps`

- `connectionOps`
- `kanban`
- `fileOps`
- `attachmentOps`

- Create RPC files under `src/server/rpc/domains/`
- Extract service modules as needed under `src/main/services/` or `src/server/services/`
- Modify matching files under `src/main/ipc/`
- Test parity per domain under `src/server/__tests__/`

- [x] Extract domain logic from IPC handler into Electron-free service functions.
- [x] Keep old IPC handler as an adapter over the extracted function during the coexistence phase.
- [x] Add RPC handler as another adapter over the same function.
- [x] Add tests that verify RPC output matches current IPC envelope behavior.
- [x] Switch the compatibility shim method by method from IPC to RPC.
- [x] Leave old IPC in place until direct renderer callers are gone, then remove it after Phase 13 deletion.

**Acceptance criteria:**

- Settings, project list, worktree list, kanban tickets, files, and attachments work through HTTP/WS.
- IPC and RPC parity tests pass during migration.

## Phase 7: Event Subscriptions

**Goal:** Replace `BrowserWindow.webContents.send` and `ipcRenderer.on` with server-published WebSocket subscriptions.

**Events to migrate:**

- `git:statusChanged`
- `git:branchChanged`
- `worktree:branchRenamed`
- `file-tree:change`
- `opencode:stream`
- `telegram:statusChanged`
- `telegram:planImplementRequested`
- `script:*`
- `terminal:data:*`
- `terminal:exit:*`
- `terminal:claude-session-id:*`
- `claude-cli:status`
- `bash:stream`

**Files:**

- Modify: `src/server/events/event-bus.ts`
- Modify: `src/server/rpc/ws-server.ts`
- Modify affected services that currently call `webContents.send`
- Test: `src/server/__tests__/subscriptions.test.ts`

- [x] Add subscription request shape: `{ channel: string; filter?: unknown }`, with explicit WebSocket subscribe control messages sent by the renderer transport and accepted by the server.
- [x] Add filtered event streams over WS by replacing connection-wide event broadcasts with per-socket channel subscriptions on the server event bus.
- [x] Add unsubscribe support with renderer-side unsubscribe control messages and server-side per-socket cleanup.
- [x] Batch terminal/script output chunks.
- [x] Replace service-level `BrowserWindow` dependencies with event bus publishing.
- [x] Keep menu/shortcut events on backend-published WebSocket channels, not `desktopBridge` IPC listeners.

**Acceptance criteria:**

- Renderer can subscribe/unsubscribe to server events.
- High-volume output does not flood the renderer with one WS frame per byte chunk.
- Reconnect can resubscribe.

- [x] `window.scriptOps.getPort(cwd)` uses RPC method `scriptOps.getPort` through the renderer compatibility layer, with the existing port registry lookup reused by the backend RPC domain so non-empty cwd validation, assigned-port lookup, null-for-unassigned behavior, and the legacy `Envelope<{ port: number | null }>` value shape are preserved.
- [x] The old `port:get` preload IPC invoke and main-process handler were removed after `window.scriptOps.getPort(cwd)`, `scriptApi.getPort(cwd)`, and `RunTab` assigned-port loading were routed through RPC method `scriptOps.getPort`.
- [x] `window.scriptOps.killPid(pid)` uses RPC method `scriptOps.killPid` through the renderer compatibility layer, with the existing PID termination logic extracted into an Electron-free service helper reused by both the legacy IPC handler and backend RPC domain so invalid PID handling, ESRCH/EPERM process probing behavior, SIGTERM then SIGKILL escalation, and the legacy `Envelope<{ killed, reason? }>` value shape are preserved.
- [x] `window.scriptOps.runArchive(commands, cwd)` uses RPC method `scriptOps.runArchive` through the renderer compatibility layer, with the existing archive command runner reused by the backend RPC domain so command/cwd validation, 30 second command timeout, combined output/error result shape, success telemetry, and the legacy `Envelope<{ success, output, error? }>` value shape are preserved.
- [x] The old `script:runArchive` preload IPC invoke and main-process handler were removed after `window.scriptOps.runArchive(commands, cwd)` was routed through RPC method `scriptOps.runArchive`.
- [x] `window.scriptOps.onOutput(channel, callback)` uses dynamic WebSocket event subscriptions through the renderer compatibility layer, with the existing script runner mirroring every `script:*` output event to the backend event endpoint while preserving output batching, long-running events, callback payload filtering, and unsubscribe behavior.
- [x] The old script-runner `webContents.send(eventKey, event)` output path was removed after script output consumers moved to `scriptApi.onOutput(...)`, the compatibility WebSocket route, and backend event publication.
- [x] The old empty `registerScriptHandlers()` startup registration and `ScriptRunner.setMainWindow()` renderer-window wiring were removed after all script invocations and output streams moved through RPC/WebSocket paths, while keeping `cleanupScripts()` for shutdown process cleanup.

- [x] Delete the old `src/main/ipc/script-handlers.ts` compatibility re-export after app shutdown and tests were retargeted to `src/main/services/script-cleanup.ts`.
- [x] The old `scriptOps.onOutput(channel, callback)` preload IPC event adapter was removed after `window.scriptOps.onOutput(channel, callback)`, `scriptApi.onOutput(channel, callback)`, `fireSetupScript()`, and `fireRunScript()` were routed through WebSocket subscriptions.
- [x] `window.scriptOps.offOutput(channel)` uses the renderer compatibility layer's WebSocket unsubscribe registry to remove all active script output subscriptions for a dynamic channel, preserving the legacy `ipcRenderer.removeAllListeners(channel)` behavior for setup/run output channels without adding a server round trip.
- [x] The old `scriptOps.offOutput(channel)` preload IPC event adapter was removed after `window.scriptOps.offOutput(channel)` used the renderer compatibility layer's WebSocket unsubscribe registry.
- [x] `window.scriptOps.runSetup(commands, cwd, worktreeId)` uses RPC method `scriptOps.runSetup` through the renderer compatibility layer, with the backend RPC domain reusing the sequential script runner, lazy port environment resolution, setup success telemetry, `script:setup:{worktreeId}` output channel, command/cwd/worktree validation, and the legacy `Envelope<{ success, error? }>` value shape.
- [x] The old `script:runSetup` preload IPC invoke and main-process handler were removed after `window.scriptOps.runSetup(commands, cwd, worktreeId)`, `scriptApi.runSetup(commands, cwd, worktreeId)`, and `fireSetupScript()` were routed through RPC method `scriptOps.runSetup`.
- [x] `window.scriptOps.kill(worktreeId)` uses RPC method `scriptOps.kill` through the renderer compatibility layer, killing backend-owned `script:run:{worktreeId}` processes first and falling back to a desktop command that reuses the legacy main-process script runner for processes started before migration, preserving non-empty worktree validation and the legacy `Envelope<{ success, error? }>` value shape.
- [x] The old `script:kill` preload IPC invoke and main-process handler were removed after `window.scriptOps.kill(worktreeId)`, `scriptApi.kill(worktreeId)`, and `killRunScript()` were routed through RPC method `scriptOps.kill`.

- [x] The old empty preload `scriptOps` global exposure was removed after every legacy `window.scriptOps` method was supplied by the renderer HTTP/WebSocket compatibility shim.
- [x] `window.terminalOps.onData(terminalId, callback)` uses a dynamic WebSocket event subscription through the renderer compatibility layer, with the terminal PTY listener publishing buffered `terminal:data:{terminalId}` string payloads to the backend event bus so current node-pty ownership and output batching behavior are preserved without renderer IPC.
- [x] `window.terminalOps.onExit(terminalId, callback)` uses a dynamic WebSocket event subscription through the renderer compatibility layer, while the legacy terminal IPC handler continues sending `terminal:exit:{terminalId}` to Electron renderers and mirrors the same numeric exit-code payload to the backend event bus so PTY cleanup, Claude CLI completion status handling, and unsubscribe behavior are preserved during the strangler migration.

- [x] `window.terminalOps.resize(terminalId, cols, rows)` uses RPC method `terminalOps.resize` through the renderer compatibility layer, with backend-owned PTYs resized directly when present and a desktop command fallback preserving legacy main-process PTY ownership during migration, including non-empty terminal id validation, numeric dimension validation, no-op missing-PTY behavior, and the legacy `Envelope<void>` value shape.
- [x] `window.terminalOps.destroy(terminalId)` uses RPC method `terminalOps.destroy` through the renderer compatibility layer, with backend-owned PTYs destroyed directly when present and a desktop command fallback reusing the legacy terminal cleanup helper so listener cleanup, output buffer cleanup, Claude watcher cleanup, no-op missing-PTY behavior, and the legacy `Envelope<void>` value shape are preserved during migration.
- [x] `window.terminalOps.write(terminalId, data)` uses RPC method `terminalOps.write` through the renderer compatibility layer without returning a promise, with backend-owned PTYs written directly when present and a desktop command fallback preserving legacy main-process PTY ownership, non-empty terminal id validation, string data validation, missing-PTY no-op behavior, and the legacy fire-and-forget return shape.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.checkForUpdate(options?)` uses RPC method `updaterOps.checkForUpdate` through the renderer compatibility layer, with a backend-to-main desktop command preserving Electron updater check behavior, optional manual-check flag forwarding, empty/options parameter validation, logged updater failure behavior, and the legacy `Envelope<void>` value shape.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.downloadUpdate()` uses RPC method `updaterOps.downloadUpdate` through the renderer compatibility layer, with a backend-to-main desktop command preserving Electron updater download behavior, empty-parameter validation, logged updater failure behavior, and the legacy `Envelope<void>` value shape.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.installUpdate()` uses RPC method `updaterOps.installUpdate` through the renderer compatibility layer, with a backend-to-main desktop command preserving Electron updater quit-and-install behavior, empty-parameter validation, and the legacy `Envelope<void>` value shape.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.setChannel(channel)` uses RPC method `updaterOps.setChannel` through the renderer compatibility layer, with a backend-to-main desktop command preserving Electron updater channel switching, `stable`/`canary` validation, internal manual update check side effect, and the legacy `Envelope<void>` value shape.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.getVersion()` uses RPC method `updaterOps.getVersion` through the renderer compatibility layer, with a backend-to-main desktop command preserving Electron app version lookup, empty-parameter validation, and the legacy `Envelope<string>` value shape.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.onChecking(callback)` uses WebSocket event `updater:checking` through the renderer compatibility layer, with the main updater service still sending the existing Electron event and also publishing the same no-payload event to the backend event bus so callback and unsubscribe behavior are preserved.
- [x] Add WebSocket subscription coverage for `updater:checking`, proving subscribed clients receive backend event-bus update-checking notifications on the local server event channel without any preload IPC listener or `webContents.send` bridge.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.onUpdateAvailable(callback)` uses WebSocket event `updater:available` through the renderer compatibility layer, with the main updater service still sending the existing Electron event and also publishing the same update metadata payload to the backend event bus so callback filtering and unsubscribe behavior are preserved.
- [x] Add WebSocket subscription coverage for `updater:available`, proving subscribed clients receive backend event-bus update-available metadata on the local server event channel without any preload IPC listener or `webContents.send` bridge.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.onUpdateNotAvailable(callback)` uses WebSocket event `updater:not-available` through the renderer compatibility layer, with the main updater service still sending the existing Electron event and also publishing the same version/manual-check payload to the backend event bus so callback filtering and unsubscribe behavior are preserved.
- [x] Add WebSocket subscription coverage for `updater:not-available`, proving subscribed clients receive backend event-bus latest-version/manual-check metadata on the local server event channel without any preload IPC listener or `webContents.send` bridge.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.onProgress(callback)` uses WebSocket event `updater:progress` through the renderer compatibility layer, with the main updater service still sending the existing Electron event and also publishing the same numeric download progress payload to the backend event bus so callback filtering and unsubscribe behavior are preserved.
- [x] Add WebSocket subscription coverage for `updater:progress`, proving subscribed clients receive backend event-bus numeric download progress payloads on the local server event channel without any preload IPC listener or `webContents.send` bridge.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.onUpdateDownloaded(callback)` uses WebSocket event `updater:downloaded` through the renderer compatibility layer, with the main updater service still sending the existing Electron event and also publishing the same version/release-notes payload to the backend event bus so callback filtering and unsubscribe behavior are preserved.
- [x] Add WebSocket subscription coverage for `updater:downloaded`, proving subscribed clients receive backend event-bus downloaded-version/release-notes payloads on the local server event channel without any preload IPC listener or `webContents.send` bridge.
- [x] `window.updaterOps.onError(callback)` uses WebSocket event `updater:error` through the renderer compatibility layer, with the main updater service still sending the existing Electron event and also publishing the same message/manual-check payload to the backend event bus so callback filtering and unsubscribe behavior are preserved.
- [x] Add WebSocket subscription coverage for `updater:error`, proving subscribed clients receive backend event-bus updater error message/manual-check payloads on the local server event channel without any preload IPC listener or `webContents.send` bridge.

**Acceptance criteria:**

- xterm terminal works in Electron and Chrome.
- Script output streams over WS.
- Ghostty absence does not break browser mode.

## Phase 10: Agent APIs

**Goal:** Move OpenCode, Claude Code, Claude CLI, and Codex session APIs to server RPC.

**Files:**

- Refactor: `src/main/ipc/opencode-handlers.ts`
- Refactor: `src/main/services/opencode-service.ts`
- Refactor: `src/main/services/agent-sdk-manager.ts`
- Refactor: `src/main/services/claude-code-implementer.ts`
- Refactor: `src/main/services/codex-implementer.ts`
- Refactor: `src/main/services/agent-event-bus.ts`
- Create: `src/server/rpc/domains/agent.ts`
- Test: `src/server/__tests__/agent-rpc.mock-provider.test.ts`
- Test: `src/server/__tests__/agent-stream-subscription.test.ts`

- [x] Remove `BrowserWindow` from core agent service dependencies.
- [x] Remove Codex implementer's retained desktop window binding; Codex pending-feedback notifications now ask `notificationService` whether the app has an unfocused main window, keeping BrowserWindow/focus state in the desktop notification service.
- [x] Remove OpenCode service's retained desktop window binding; OpenCode session-complete and pending-feedback notifications now use `notificationService.shouldNotifyWhenWindowUnfocused()` instead of storing renderer window state.
- [x] Remove Claude Code implementer's retained desktop window binding; Claude Code completion and pending-feedback notifications now use `notificationService.shouldNotifyWhenWindowUnfocused()` instead of storing renderer window state.
- [x] Remove the now-unused `AgentMainWindowState` and `AgentSdkManager.setMainWindow(...)` plumbing after all agent implementations stopped retaining desktop window state.
- [x] Publish agent streams through server event bus; `agentEventBus.publish(...)` posts `opencode:stream` events to the local backend event endpoint, and subscribed WebSocket clients receive the same stream payload.
- [x] Add mocked-provider RPC coverage for `opencodeOps.connect`, proving the router validates params before calling the injected agent provider and returns the provider result over RPC without touching Electron IPC.
- [x] Add mocked-provider RPC coverage for `opencodeOps.reconnect`, proving the router validates params before calling the injected agent provider and returns reconnect status/revert metadata over RPC without touching Electron IPC.

## Phase 12: Renderer API Cleanup

**Goal:** Stop relying on `window.*Ops` globals in app code.

**Files:**

- Modify renderer stores and hooks under `src/renderer/src/stores/`
- Modify renderer components under `src/renderer/src/components/`
- Deleted: `src/renderer/src/api/legacy-window-api.ts`
- Modify: `src/preload/index.ts`
- Modify: `src/preload/index.d.ts`

- [x] Introduce explicit API access hooks or modules for each domain.
- [x] `systemApi.isPackaged()` provides an explicit renderer API module for RPC method `systemOps.isPackaged`, and `useCommands` no longer calls the `window.systemOps.isPackaged()` compatibility global directly.
- [x] `systemApi.openInChrome(url, customCommand?)` provides an explicit renderer API module for RPC method `systemOps.openInChrome`, and `useLifecycleActions.openPRInBrowser` no longer calls the `window.systemOps.openInChrome()` compatibility global directly.
- [x] `RunOutputLine` URL Cmd/Ctrl-click handling uses `systemApi.openInChrome(url, customCommand?)` instead of the `window.systemOps.openInChrome()` compatibility global, preserving custom Chrome command forwarding and click filtering.
- [x] `BottomPanel` dev-server URL opening uses `systemApi.openInChrome(detectedUrl, customCommand?)` instead of the `window.systemOps.openInChrome()` compatibility global, preserving custom Chrome command forwarding and right-click configuration behavior.
- [x] `PinnedList` attachment URL opening uses `systemApi.openInChrome(url)` instead of the `window.systemOps.openInChrome()` compatibility global, preserving the awaited browser-open behavior for pinned worktree attachments.
- [x] `WorktreeItem` attachment URL opening uses `systemApi.openInChrome(url)` instead of the `window.systemOps.openInChrome()` compatibility global, preserving the awaited browser-open behavior for worktree attachments.
- [x] `KanbanTicketModal` external ticket URL opening uses `systemApi.openInChrome(ticket.external_url!)` instead of the `window.systemOps.openInChrome()` compatibility global, preserving the fire-and-forget provider-link button behavior.

**Acceptance criteria:**

- Core renderer code has no direct dependency on Electron IPC globals.
- Only `desktopBridge` remains as a window global.

---

## Phase 13: IPC Deletion

**Goal:** Remove old business IPC handlers and preload namespaces.

**Files:**

- Delete migrated files under `src/main/ipc/` where no longer needed.
- Shrink: `src/preload/index.ts`
- Shrink: `src/preload/index.d.ts`
- Update: `README.md`
- Update architecture docs.

- [x] Delete migrated IPC handlers.
- [x] Delete old preload namespace exposure for business APIs.
- [x] Delete old IPC-specific tests or convert them to RPC tests.
- [x] Update README architecture diagram from IPC to HTTP/WS.
- [x] Run full build/test/lint suite.

**Acceptance criteria:**

- No core application operation uses Electron IPC.
- Electron IPC is desktop-shell-only.
- Server can run headlessly.
- Chrome can run Hive against the backend.

---

## Testing Strategy

Required test categories:

- Server config tests.
- Auth bootstrap tests.
- RPC router tests.
- WebSocket transport tests.
- Domain parity tests while IPC and RPC coexist.
- Subscription tests.
- Temp git repository integration tests.
- Terminal PTY integration tests.
- Script streaming tests.
- Mocked agent provider tests.
- Electron smoke test.
- Browser Playwright smoke test.

Recommended verification commands during implementation:

```bash
pnpm test
pnpm build
pnpm lint
pnpm test:e2e
```

Run narrower tests at each phase before running the full suite.

---

## First Milestone

Build the smallest useful vertical slice:

- Desktop starts backend.
- Backend exposes health route and `/ws`.
- Renderer authenticates using desktop bootstrap.
- RPC supports:
  - `db.setting.get`
  - `db.setting.set`
  - `db.setting.getAll`
- Compatibility shim exposes existing `window.db.setting`.
- Existing settings flow works through WS.
- Chrome can open the Vite app and connect to the backend.

This proves the architecture before migrating the full IPC surface.

---

## Migration Risks

- The current preload exposes a very large API surface, so compatibility shim behavior must be precise.
- Agent streams and approval flows are the highest-risk migration area.
- Terminal streaming needs batching and reconnect behavior.
- Browser file uploads cannot rely on Electron `webUtils.getPathForFile`.
- Ghostty native surfaces cannot work in Chrome and must remain optional.
- A local backend has filesystem/git/terminal privileges, so auth cannot be deferred.

---

## Completion Definition

The migration is complete when:

- Electron app works as before.
- Chrome can run Hive against the backend.
- Server owns all business logic.
- Renderer uses HTTP/WS client APIs.
- `src/preload/index.ts` exposes only desktop shell functionality.
- Old business IPC handlers are removed.
- Full verification suite passes.
